Usage\n       </h2>\n       <p>\n        If you just need a simple modal, you can use the\n        <code>\n         title\n        </code>\n        prop and the default footer. class="bs-docs-section" id="form-group">\n       <h1 class="page-header">\n        <a class="anchor" href="#form-group">\n         Form Group\n        </a>\n       </h1>\n       <p>\n        This is not a style component, is just a global validation manager.\n       </p>\n       <p>\n        If you need to evaluate if a group of elements are all valids, you can handle easier with this component.\n       </p>\n       <p>\n        In this example, the buttons and tabs are disabled while the inner elements are empty.\n       </p>\n       <div class="bs-example">\n        <div class="row">\n         <div class="col-xs-12 col-sm-12 col-md-4 col-lg-4">\n          <p>\n          </p>\n          <pre>Valid user data : false</pre>\n          <p>\n          </p>\n    <div class="col-xs-12 col-sm-12 col-md-4 col-lg-4">\n          <p>\n          </p>\n          <pre>All valid : false</pre>\n          <p>\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n        <div class="row">\n         <!--v-start-->\n         <div class="col-xs-12 col-sm-12 col-md-12 col-lg-12">\n          <!--v-start-->\n          <ul _v-9a9541e6="" class="nav nav-tabs"
